***решка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:решка.html>ре́шка</a> (26290)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:решетка.html>решётка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rešótka</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lattice, grid</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:решето.html>решето́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rešetó</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sieve</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, probably referring to the royal monogram on one side of some 18th century Russian coins.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:решка.html>ре́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">réška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:решка.html>ре́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:решка.html>ре́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:решка.html>ре́шек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tails <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">the side of a coin <i>not</i> bearing a coat of arms</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">орёл <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>и́ли</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:решка.html>ре́шка</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">orjól íli <b>réška</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">heads or <b>tails</b>?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The terms <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">орёл</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">orjól</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:решка.html>ре́шка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">réška</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are applicable only to coins which, like Russia's coinage, have a coat of arms on one side and something else (e.g. the portrait of the head of state or the value of the coin) on the other. The terms <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">аве́рс</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">avérs</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ре́верс</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">révers</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are more universally applicable, but used mainly in numismatics.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">heads</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">аве́рс</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">avérs</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">tails</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ре́верс</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">révers</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3*a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***реять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:реять.html>ре́ять</a> (21046)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">рѣяти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rějati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">рѣѩти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rějęti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">рі́яти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ríjaty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg"><a href = vnd.unilang:рея.html>ре́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сё</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">réja se</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">raĩdît</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">रेतस्</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rétas</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Deva mention" <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">रयते</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rī́уаte</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">रिणाति</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">riṇā́ti</span><span <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реять.html>ре́ять</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">réjatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ри́нуть</b>)

<ol><li>to soar, to fly, to hover</li>
<li>to flutter, to fly (of a flag)</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ржавый.html>ржа́в</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>чи<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b>

Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-рж-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-ав-чин</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ръжавъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rŭžavŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rъďavъ</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rъďa</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-avъ</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ржать.html>ржа</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rža</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ávyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ржать.html>ржать</a> (11370)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ръзати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rŭzati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*rewǵ-</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ржать.html>ржать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ržatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заржать.html>заржа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to neigh
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лошадь.html>ло́шадь</a> <strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:ржать.html>ржёт</a></strong></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lóšadʹ ržót</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a horse neighs</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to laugh
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ржать.html>ржёт</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ržot!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">lol!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ржать.html>ржать</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***риза.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:риза.html>ри́за</a> (30007)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*riza</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:риск.html>риск</a> (3366)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:риск.html>риск</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">risk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:риск.html>ри́ска</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:риск.html>ри́ски</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:риск.html>ри́сков</a></b>)

***рискованный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рискованный.html>риско́ванный</a> (8112)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Constructed as if the past passive participle of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рисковать.html>рискова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">riskovátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to risk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рискованный.html>риско́ванный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">riskóvannyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>risky, dodgy</li>
<li>risque</li></ol>

***рисковый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рисковый.html>риско́вый</a> (25332)</h1><br><hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>ри<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ско́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:выя.html>вы́й</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>риско́вее, риско́вей.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-риск-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ов</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рисование.html>рисова́ние</a> (16112)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рисовать.html>рисова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">risovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рисование.html>рисова́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">risovánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рисование.html>рисова́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рисование.html>рисова́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рисование.html>рисова́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>drawing <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">act of producing a picture</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>ри<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>е</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 7a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> словообразования: рисованье.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-рис-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-ова-ниj</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-е</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***рисовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рисовать.html>рисова́ть</a> (2959)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">rysować</i>, from Middle High German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">rīzen</i>, whence also German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">reißen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рисовать.html>рисова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">risovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нарисовать.html>нарисова́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to draw, to design</li>
<li>to paint</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рисовать.html>рисова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">risovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<ol><li>to be silhouetted</li>
<li>to present itself <i>(to)</i>

<li>to pose, to show off</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рисовать.html>рисова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">risovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рис.html>рис</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ris</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рисовый.html>ри́совый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rísovyj</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)

<p><b>ри<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:су.html>су́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>нок</b>
